A.JIWON_MM -- 지원월 , A.GEUNROJA_NO -- 근로자번호 , A.SIMSA_CNT -- 심사회차 , A.JIGEUP_JEOPSU_NO -- 지급접수번호 , A.JIGEUP_GJ_DT -- 지급결정일자 , A.JIWON_PRC_SANJENG_PRC -- 지원금산정금액 , A.GAMSI_DANSOK_YN -- 감시단속여부 , AS GENDER -- 성별 , CASE WHEN A.RGNO_GENDER IN ('1','2','3','4','9','0') THEN '1' WHEN A.RGNO_GENDER IN ('5','6','7','8') THEN '9' ELSE '' END AS GUKJEOK -- 국적 , CASE WHEN A.RGNO_DT IS NOT NULL THEN FLOOR(MONTHS_BETWEEN(TO_DATE(A.JEOPSU_DT, 'YYYYMMDD') , TO_DATE(A.RGNO_DT, 'YYYYMMDD')) / 12 ) ELSE 0 END AS AGE -- 연령 , A.GEUNROJA_FG -- 근로자구분 , A.MM_AVG_BOSU_PRC -- 월평균보수 , 'N' -- 최초여부 , A.DAENAP_YN LEFT OUTER JOIN IJA090MT C ON C.ILJARI_NO = A.ILJARI_NO AND C.BOGO_YYMM = (CASE WHEN SUBSTR(A.JIGEUP_DT,1,6) <= '201803' THEN '201803' ELSE (SELECT MAX(BOGO_YYMM) FROM IJA090MT WHERE BOGO_YYMM <= SUBSTR(A.JIGEUP_DT,1,6)) END) -- 기업정보 마스터(고용보험관리번호) LEFT OUTER JOIN IJA010MT D1 ON D1.ILJARI_NO = A.DAEPYO_ILJARI_NO -- 기업정보 디테일(고용보험관련정보) LEFT OUTER JOIN IJA013DT D ON D.ILJARI_NO = A.DAEPYO_ILJARI_NO -- 우편번호 지역 및 노동부 지청 정보. LEFT OUTER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT TRIM(Z.POST) AS POST, Z.SIDO, Z2.SIGUNGU AS SS, Z2.SIGUNGU_TITLE AS SIGUNGU, Z3.CENTER_CD AS JICHEONG_CD, Z3.JICHUNG_NM AS JICHEONG_NAME FROM IZA078CT Z LEFT OUTER JOIN IZA079CT Z2 ON Z2.SIGUNGU = SUBSTR(Z.POST, 1,3) AND Z2.SIGUNGU_FG = '4' LEFT OUTER JOIN IQZ080CT Z3 ON Z3.SIDO = Z.SIDO AND Z3.CENTER_CD = Z.CENTER_CD AND NVL(Z3.SIGUNGU, 'Z') = NVL(Z.SIGUNGU, 'Z') ) E ON E.POST = A.SAEOPJANG_POST -- 민원서류코드 LEFT OUTER JOIN (SELECT B.ILJARI_NO, MAX(A.MINWON_DOC_CD) AS MINWON_DOC_CD FROM IQA500MT A INNER JOIN IAA010MT B ON B.JEOPSU_NO = A.JEOPSU_NO WHERE A.MINWON_DOC_CD IN ('6001','6002','6003','6004','6005') AND A.JEOPSU_STATUS_CD = '3' AND A.GYEOLJAE_STATUS_CD = '3' GROUP BY B.ILJARI_NO ) F ON F.ILJARI_NO = A.ILJARI_NO -- 고용보험 디테일(적용제외근로자여부) LEFT OUTER JOIN IJA113DT G ON A.GEUNROJA_FG = '01' AND G.GEUNROJA_NO = A.GEUNROJA_NO AND G.ILJARI_NO = A.DAEPYO_ILJARI_NO AND A.JIWON_YEAR || A.JIWON_MM BETWEEN SUBSTR(G.GY_JAGYEOK_CHWIDEUK_DT, 1, 6) AND NVL(SUBSTR(G.GY_JAGYEOK_SANGSIL_DT,1,6), '299912') AND G.SNO = (SELECT MAX(SNO) FROM IJA113DT G1 WHERE A.GEUNROJA_FG = '01' AND G1.GEUNROJA_NO = A.GEUNROJA_NO AND G1.ILJARI_NO = A.DAEPYO_ILJARI_NO AND A.JIWON_YEAR || A.JIWON_MM BETWEEN SUBSTR(G1.GY_JAGYEOK_CHWIDEUK_DT, 1, 6) AND NVL(SUBSTR(G1.GY_JAGYEOK_SANGSIL_DT,1,6), '299912') ) LEFT OUTER JOIN IJA115DT H ON A.GEUNROJA_FG = '02' AND H.GEUNROJA_NO = A.GEUNROJA_NO AND H.ILJARI_NO = A.DAEPYO_ILJARI_NO AND H.DAESANG_YYMM = A.JIWON_YEAR || A.JIWON_MM AND H.SNO = 1

SAEOPJA_DRNO , JIGEUP_HUIMANG_IL , GWANRI_JISA_CD , FIRST_JEOPSU_NO , FIRST_MINWON_DOC_CD , SER , CHANGE_JEOPSU_NO , CHANGE_MINWON_DOC_CD , JAESIMSA_DAESANG_YN , JAESIMSA_FG_CD , JAESIMSA_COMPLETE_YN , JAESIMSA_COMPLETE_DT , JAESIMSA_JIGEUP_NO , JIWON_JUNGJI_STATUS_CD , JIWON_JUNGJI_SAYU_CD , JIWON_JUNGJI_FROM_DT , JIWON_JUNGJI_HAEJI_DT , JIWON_YEAR , JIWON_MM , JEONGGI_CNT , SIMSA_CNT , A.DAEPYO_ILJARI_NO AS DAEPYO_ILJARI_NO , A.ILJARI_NO , A.GYB_GWANRI_NO , A.SAEOPJANG_NM , A.P_NM AS P_DAEPYOJA_NM , CASE WHEN A.SAEOPJANG_FG IN ('2','3') THEN 'Y' ELSE '' END AS GONGDONGJUTAEK_YUHYEONG_CD , A.DURUNURI_JIWON_YN , A.SAEOPJA_DRNO , A.JIGEUP_HUIMANG_IL , A.GWANRI_JISA_CD , A.JEOPSU_NO AS FIRST_JEOPSU_NO , Q2.MINWON_DOC_CD AS FIRST_MINWON_DOC_CD , B.SER , B.CHANGE_JEOPSU_NO , Q1.MINWON_DOC_CD AS CHANGE_MINWON_DOC_CD , B.JAESIMSA_DAESANG_YN , B.JAESIMSA_FG_CD , B.JAESIMSA_COMPLETE_YN , B.JAESIMSA_COMPLETE_DT , B.JAESIMSA_JIGEUP_NO , BULSEUNGIN_SAYU_CD , C.SIKBYEOL_NO , E.JY_DAMDANGJA_ID AS DAMDANGJA_ID , D.DAESANG_YN FROM IAA190MT B INNER JOIN IJB050MT C ON C.ILJARI_NO = B.ILJARI_NO AND C.JEONGGI_JIGEUP_DT = '2018' || '05' || '20' /* AND B.JIWON_JUNGJI_FROM_DT <= C.JEONGGI_JIGEUP_DT 2018.04.23 문형수K요청으로 조건추가 */ AND C.JEONGGI_JIGEUP_DT BETWEEN B.JIWON_JUNGJI_FROM_DT AND B.JIWON_JUNGJI_HAEJI_DT /* 2018.05.11 문형수K요청으로 조건추가 */ 0) AS TOT_SINCHEONG_CNT , nvl(SUM(A1.SC_CNT1), 0) + nvl(sum(A1.SC_CNT2), 0) + nvl(sum(A1.SC_CNT3), 0) + nvl(sum(A1.SC_CNT4), 0) AS TOT_GEUNROJA_CNT , nvl(SUM(A1.SJ_CNT1), 0) AS SAEOPJANG_CNT1 , B.SAEOPJA_DRNO), G.P_MINWONIN_RGNO ) AS SAEOPJANG_GIJUN_NO , B.SAEOPJANG_POST , min( case when 1=1 then (select case when count(distinct GEUNROJA_NO) < 5 then '0004' when count(distinct GEUNROJA_NO) < 10 then '0509' when count(distinct GEUNROJA_NO) < 30 then '1030' else 'more' end from IJA113DT where ILJARI_NO = B.ILJARI_NO and GY_STATUS_CD in ('0', '2')) end) as GYUMO_STR , MAX( CASE WHEN A.GEUNROJA_FG = '01' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS SANGYONG_CNT , CASE WHEN JEOE_GEUNROJA_FG = 2 AND A.GEUNROJA_FG = '02' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS ILYONG_CNT , CASE WHEN JEOE_GEUNROJA_FG = 1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS JEOE_CNT , CASE WHEN A.AGE = 0 THEN '연령오류' WHEN A.AGE < 20 THEN '20대 미만' WHEN A.AGE < 30 THEN '20대' WHEN A.AGE < 40 THEN '30대' WHEN A.AGE < 50 THEN '40대' WHEN A.AGE < 60 THEN '50대' ELSE '60대 이상' END AS AGE_FG , CASE WHEN A.AGE = 0 THEN '7' WHEN A.AGE < 20 THEN '1' WHEN A.AGE < 30 THEN '2' WHEN A.AGE < 40 THEN '3' WHEN A.AGE < 50 THEN '4' WHEN A.AGE < 60 THEN '5' ELSE '6' END AS AGE_SORT , CASE WHEN A.MAX_JIWON_PRC_SANJENG_PRC = 130000 THEN '13만원' WHEN A.MAX_JIWON_PRC_SANJENG_PRC >= 120000 THEN '12만원이상-13만원미만' WHEN A.MAX_JIWON_PRC_SANJENG_PRC >= 100000 THEN '10만원이상-12만원미만' WHEN A.MAX_JIWON_PRC_SANJENG_PRC >= 90000 THEN '9만원이상-10만원미만' WHEN A.MAX_JIWON_PRC_SANJENG_PRC >= 60000 THEN '6만원이상-9만원미만' WHEN A.MAX_JIWON_PRC_SANJENG_PRC >= 30000 THEN '3만원이상-6만원미만' ELSE '3만원미만' END AS A.MAX_JIWON_PRC_SANJENG_PRC >= 90000 THEN '4' WHEN A.MAX_JIWON_PRC_SANJENG_PRC >= 60000 THEN '5' WHEN A.MAX_JIWON_PRC_SANJENG_PRC >= 30000 THEN '6' ELSE '7' END AS MAX_JIWON_PRC_SORT , CASE WHEN A.AVG_JIWON_PRC_SANJENG_PRC = 130000 THEN '13만원' WHEN A.AVG_JIWON_PRC_SANJENG_PRC >= 120000 THEN '12만원이상-13만원미만' WHEN A.AVG_JIWON_PRC_SANJENG_PRC >= 100000 THEN '10만원이상-12만원미만' WHEN A.AVG_JIWON_PRC_SANJENG_PRC >= 90000 THEN '9만원이상-10만원미만' WHEN A.AVG_JIWON_PRC_SANJENG_PRC >= 60000 THEN '6만원이상-9만원미만' WHEN A.AVG_JIWON_PRC_SANJENG_PRC >= 30000 THEN '3만원이상-6만원미만' ELSE '3만원미만' END AS AVG_JIWON_PRC_FG , CASE WHEN A.AVG_JIWON_PRC_SANJENG_PRC = 130000 THEN '1' WHEN A.AVG_JIWON_PRC_SANJENG_PRC >= 120000 THEN '2' WHEN A.AVG_JIWON_PRC_SANJENG_PRC >= 100000 THEN '3' WHEN A.AVG_JIWON_PRC_SANJENG_PRC >= 90000 THEN '4' WHEN A.AVG_JIWON_PRC_SANJENG_PRC >= 60000 THEN '5' WHEN A.AVG_JIWON_PRC_SANJENG_PRC >= 30000 THEN '6' ELSE '7' END AS AVG_JIWON_PRC_SORT , CASE WHEN NVL(A.GY_SANGSI_INWON_CNT,0) = 0 THEN '기타' WHEN NVL(A.GY_SANGSI_INWON_CNT,0) < 5 THEN '5인미만' WHEN NVL(A.GY_SANGSI_INWON_CNT,0) < 10 THEN '5-9인' WHEN NVL(A.GY_SANGSI_INWON_CNT,0) < 30 THEN '10-29인' WHEN NVL(A.GY_SANGSI_INWON_CNT,0) >= 30 THEN '30인이상' ELSE '기타' END AS GY_SANGSI_INWON_FG , CASE WHEN NVL(A.GY_SANGSI_INWON_CNT,0) = 0 THEN '5' WHEN NVL(A.GY_SANGSI_INWON_CNT,0) < 5 THEN '1' WHEN NVL(A.GY_SANGSI_INWON_CNT,0) < 10 THEN '2' WHEN NVL(A.GY_SANGSI_INWON_CNT,0) < 30 THEN '3' WHEN NVL(A.GY_SANGSI_INWON_CNT,0) >= 30 THEN '4' ELSE '5' END AS GY_SANGSI_INWON_SORT FROM ( SELECT ILJARI_NO, GEUNROJA_NO, GWANRI_JISA_CD, GY_EOPJONG_CD, JEOE_GEUNROJA_FG , DAENAP_YN, DAEPYO_ILJARI_NO , SUBSTR(MAX(MAX_GEUNROJA_FG), 9, 2) AS GEUNROJA_FG , MAX(AGE) AS AGE , MAX(GY_SANGSI_INWON_CNT) AS GY_SANGSI_INWON_CNT , MAX(JIWON_PRC_SANJENG_PRC) AS MAX_JIWON_PRC_SANJENG_PRC , AVG(JIWON_PRC_SANJENG_PRC) AS AVG_JIWON_PRC_SANJENG_PRC , SUM(JIWON_PRC_SANJENG_PRC) AS JIWON_PRC_SANJENG_PRC FROM ( SELECT A.JIGEUP_DT , A.JISA_CD , A.JIGEUP_SER , A.ILJARI_NO , A.DAENAP_YN , A.JIWON_YEAR , A.JIWON_MM , A.GEUNROJA_NO , A.JIWON_PRC_SANJENG_PRC , A.GEUNROJA_FG , A.MAX_GEUNROJA_FG , A.DAEPYO_ILJARI_NO , A.GWANRI_JISA_CD , B.SAEOPJANG_POST , B1.MINWON_DOC_CD , NVL(NVL(C.P_RGNO, C1.P_RGNO), D.P_RGNO) AS P_RGNO , E.GY_STATUS_CD , F.GY_GEUNRO_ILSU , G.GY_EOPJONG_CD , DECODE(B1.MINWON_DOC_CD, '6004', NVL2(G.ILJARI_NO, 2, 1), 2) AS JEOE_SAEOPJANG_FG -- 1 제외사업장 , DECODE(GEUNROJA_FG, '02', DECODE(B1.MINWON_DOC_CD, '6004', DECODE(NVL(F.GEUNROJA_NO, 'X'), 'X', 1, 2), 2), DECODE(B1.MINWON_DOC_CD, '6004', DECODE(NVL(E.GY_STATUS_CD, 'X'), '0', 2, 1), 2)) AS JEOE_GEUNROJA_FG , CASE WHEN SF_ZA_CHK_DATE(CONCAT(TO_CHAR(CASE WHEN SUBSTR(NVL(NVL(C.P_RGNO, C1.P_RGNO), D.P_RGNO), 7, 1) IN ('1','2','5','6') THEN TO_NUMBER(SUBSTR(NVL(NVL(C.P_RGNO, C1.P_RGNO), D.P_RGNO), 1, 2)) + 1900 WHEN SUBSTR(NVL(NVL(C.P_RGNO, C1.P_RGNO), D.P_RGNO), 7, 1) IN ('3','4','7','8') THEN TO_NUMBER(SUBSTR(NVL(NVL(C.P_RGNO, C1.P_RGNO), D.P_RGNO), 1, 2)) + 2000 ELSE TO_NUMBER(SUBSTR(NVL(NVL(C.P_RGNO, C1.P_RGNO), D.P_RGNO), 1, 2)) + 1800 END), SUBSTR(NVL(NVL(C.P_RGNO, C1.P_RGNO), D.P_RGNO), 3, 4))) = '1' THEN FLOOR(MONTHS_BETWEEN(TO_DATE(NVL(E.JEOPSU_DT, A.JIGEUP_HUIMANG_YYMM||'01'), 'YYYYMMDD'), TO_DATE(CONCAT(TO_CHAR(CASE WHEN SUBSTR(NVL(NVL(C.P_RGNO, C1.P_RGNO), D.P_RGNO), 7, 1) IN ('1','2','5','6') THEN TO_NUMBER(SUBSTR(NVL(NVL(C.P_RGNO, C1.P_RGNO), D.P_RGNO), 1, 2)) + 1900 WHEN SUBSTR(NVL(NVL(C.P_RGNO, C1.P_RGNO), D.P_RGNO), 7, 1) IN ('3','4','7','8') THEN TO_NUMBER(SUBSTR(NVL(NVL(C.P_RGNO, C1.P_RGNO), D.P_RGNO), 1, 2)) + 2000 ELSE TO_NUMBER(SUBSTR(NVL(NVL(C.P_RGNO, C1.P_RGNO), D.P_RGNO), 1, 2)) + 1800 END), SUBSTR(NVL(NVL(C.P_RGNO, C1.P_RGNO), D.P_RGNO), 3, 4)),'YYYYMMDD') ) / 12 ) ELSE 0 END AS AGE -- 나이 , H.GY_SANGSI_INWON_CNT FROM ( SELECT A.FBS_JIGEUP_DT AS JIGEUP_DT -- 지급일 , A.JISA_CD , A.JIGEUP_SER , A.ILJARI_NO , A.DAENAP_YN , B.JEOPSU_NO , B.JIWON_YEAR , B.JIWON_MM , C.GEUNROJA_NO , C.JIWON_PRC_SANJENG_PRC , C.GEUNROJA_FG , D.JIGEUP_HUIMANG_YYMM , D.DAEPYO_ILJARI_NO , E.GWANRI_JISA_CD , E.JEOPSU_DT||C.GEUNROJA_FG AS MAX_GEUNROJA_FG FROM IBC250MT A -- 펌뱅킹지급의뢰 INNER JOIN IBB010MT B -- 신청사업장산정 ON B.ILJARI_NO = A.ILJARI_NO AND B.JIGEUP_JEOPSU_NO = A.JEOPSU_NO INNER JOIN IBB020MT C -- 신청근로자산정 ON C.JEOPSU_NO = B.JEOPSU_NO AND C.ILJARI_NO = B.ILJARI_NO AND C.JIWON_YEAR = B.JIWON_YEAR AND C.JIWON_MM = B.JIWON_MM AND C.SIMSA_CNT = B.SIMSA_CNT AND C.JIWON_PRC_SANJENG_PRC > 0 INNER JOIN IAA100MT D ON D.ILJARI_NO = B.ILJARI_NO INNER JOIN IQA500MT E ON E.JEOPSU_NO = B.JEOPSU_NO AND E.GYEOLJAE_STATUS_CD = '3' WHERE A.FBS_JIGEUP_UIROE_FG = '2' -- 펌뱅킹지급의뢰구분 : 정상지급 AND A.FBS_JIGEUP_RESULT_CD = '0000' AND A.JIGEUP_CHEORI_FG IN ('10','11') -- 지급처리구분 : 신규, 추가 AND A.FBS_JIGEUP_DT BETWEEN '20180101' AND '20180430' -- AND E.GWANRI_JISA_CD = '2000' -- AND A.JEOPSU_NO IN ('20002018FA00058', '70012018FA00050') /* 하드코딩 부분 */ AND CASE WHEN A.JEOPSU_NO IN ('20002018FA00058', '70012018FA00050') THEN CASE WHEN A.FBS_JIGEUP_DT = '20180201' AND C.GEUNROJA_NO IN ('00001191598','00002636956','00003970759','00006767175','00007369705','00009376602','00015558226','00004490205') THEN 1 WHEN A.FBS_JIGEUP_DT = '20180202' AND C.GEUNROJA_NO IN ('00000744554','00001011891','00002900669','00002539269','00000353585') THEN 1 ELSE 0 END WHEN A.JEOPSU_NO IN ('70012018FA00096') THEN CASE WHEN A.JIGEUP_SER = 63 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END ELSE 1 END = 1 ) A INNER JOIN IAA100MT B ON B.ILJARI_NO = A.ILJARI_NO INNER JOIN (SELECT B.ILJARI_NO , MAX(A.MINWON_DOC_CD) AS MINWON_DOC_CD FROM IQA500MT A INNER JOIN IAA010MT B ON B.JEOPSU_NO = A.JEOPSU_NO WHERE A.MINWON_DOC_CD IN ('6001','6002','6003','6004','6005') AND A.JEOPSU_STATUS_CD = '3' AND A.GYEOLJAE_STATUS_CD = '3' GROUP BY B.ILJARI_NO ) B1 ON B1.ILJARI_NO = A.ILJARI_NO LEFT OUTER JOIN IAA130MT C ON C.JEOPSU_NO = A.JEOPSU_NO AND C.ILJARI_NO = A.ILJARI_NO AND C.GEUNROJA_NO = A.GEUNROJA_NO LEFT OUTER JOIN IAA030MT C1 ON C1.JEOPSU_NO = A.JEOPSU_NO AND C1.ILJARI_NO = A.ILJARI_NO AND C1.GEUNROJA_NO = A.GEUNROJA_NO LEFT OUTER JOIN IAA120MT D ON D.JEOPSU_NO = A.JEOPSU_NO AND D.ILJARI_NO = A.ILJARI_NO AND D.GEUNROJA_NO = A.GEUNROJA_NO AND D.GEUNRO_YYMM = A.JIWON_YEAR || A.JIWON_MM LEFT OUTER JOIN IJA113DT E ON E.GEUNROJA_NO = A.GEUNROJA_NO AND E.ILJARI_NO = A.ILJARI_NO AND E.GY_STATUS_CD = '0' LEFT OUTER JOIN IJA115DT F ON F.GEUNROJA_NO = A.GEUNROJA_NO AND F.ILJARI_NO = A.ILJARI_NO AND F.DAESANG_YYMM = A.JIWON_YEAR || A.JIWON_MM LEFT OUTER JOIN IJA013DT G ON G.ILJARI_NO = A.DAEPYO_ILJARI_NO -- 상시근로자수. 2018년3월부터는 IJA090MT 테이블 이용가능. LEFT OUTER JOIN IJA090MT H ON H.ILJARI_NO = A.DAEPYO_ILJARI_NO AND H.BOGO_YYMM = (CASE WHEN SUBSTR(A.JIGEUP_DT,1,6) <= '201803' THEN '201803' ELSE (SELECT MAX(BOGO_YYMM) FROM IJA090MT WHERE BOGO_YYMM <= SUBSTR(A.JIGEUP_DT,1,6)) END) ) GROUP BY ILJARI_NO, GEUNROJA_NO, GWANRI_JISA_CD, GY_EOPJONG_CD, JEOE_GEUNROJA_FG, DAENAP_YN, DAEPYO_ILJARI_NO ) A LEFT OUTER JOIN IZA021CT B ON B.GT_GROUP_CD = 'R0043' AND B.GT_CD = A.GWANRI_JISA_CD LEFT OUTER JOIN IZA040CT C ON C.GY_EOPJONG_FG = '5'AND C.GY_EOPJONG_CD = A.GY_EOPJONG_CD LEFT OUTER JOIN IZA040CT D ON D.GY_EOPJONG_FG = '1'AND D.GY_EOPJONG_CD = C.GY_EOPJONG_DAEBUNRYU_FG ) SELECT '1' AS GUBUN , '나이' AS GUBUN_NM , AGE_SORT AS SEBU_GUBUN , AGE_FG AS SEBU_GUBUN_NM , SUM(SANGYONG_CNT) AS SANGYONG_CNT , SUM(ILYONG_CNT) AS ILYONG_CNT , SUM(JEOE_CNT) AS JEOE_CNT FROM TBL_A A GROUP BY AGE_SORT, AGE_FG UNION SELECT '2' AS GUBUN , '지역' AS GUBUN_NM , GWANRI_JISA_CD AS SEBU_GUBUN , GWANRI_JISA_NM AS SEBU_GUBUN_NM , SUM(SANGYONG_CNT) AS SANGYONG_CNT , SUM(ILYONG_CNT) AS ILYONG_CNT , SUM(JEOE_CNT) AS JEOE_CNT FROM TBL_A A GROUP BY GWANRI_JISA_CD, GWANRI_JISA_NM UNION SELECT '3' AS GUBUN , '업종' AS GUBUN_NM , GY_EOPJONG_DAEBUNRYU_FG , GY_EOPJONG_DAEBUNRYU_NM , SUM(SANGYONG_CNT) AS SANGYONG_CNT , SUM(ILYONG_CNT) AS ILYONG_CNT , SUM(JEOE_CNT) AS JEOE_CNT FROM TBL_A A GROUP BY GY_EOPJONG_DAEBUNRYU_FG, GY_EOPJONG_DAEBUNRYU_NM UNION SELECT '4' AS GUBUN , '최대지원액' AS GUBUN_NM , MAX_JIWON_PRC_SORT , MAX_JIWON_PRC_FG , SUM(SANGYONG_CNT) AS SANGYONG_CNT , SUM(ILYONG_CNT) AS ILYONG_CNT , SUM(JEOE_CNT) AS JEOE_CNT FROM TBL_A A GROUP BY MAX_JIWON_PRC_SORT, MAX_JIWON_PRC_FG UNION SELECT '5' AS GUBUN , '평균지원액' AS GUBUN_NM , AVG_JIWON_PRC_SORT , AVG_JIWON_PRC_FG , SUM(SANGYONG_CNT) AS SANGYONG_CNT , SUM(ILYONG_CNT) AS ILYONG_CNT , SUM(JEOE_CNT) AS JEOE_CNT FROM TBL_A A GROUP BY AVG_JIWON_PRC_SORT, AVG_JIWON_PRC_FG UNION SELECT '6' AS GUBUN , '인원규모' AS GUBUN_NM , GY_SANGSI_INWON_SORT AS SEBU_GUBUN , GY_SANGSI_INWON_FG AS SEBU_GUBUN_NM , SUM(SANGYONG_CNT) AS SANGYONG_CNT , SUM(ILYONG_CNT) AS ILYONG_CNT , SUM(JEOE_CNT) AS JEOE_CNT FROM TBL_A A GROUP BY GY_SANGSI_INWON_SORT,GY_SANGSI_INWON_FG --ORDER BY GUBUN, GUBUN_NM, GY_SANGSI_INWON_SORT ORDER BY GUBUN, GUBUN_NM, SEBU_GUBUN

SELECT CASE WHEN T_ALL = T_CNT1 THEN '01' -- 전부 승인이면 승인 WHEN T_ALL = T_CNT2 THEN '02' -- 전부 불승인이면 불승인 WHEN T_CNT3 > 0 THEN '03' -- 보류 1개이상시 보류 WHEN T_CNT4 > 0 THEN '90' -- 반려 1개이상시 반려 WHEN MINWON_DOC_CD <> '6003' AND T_CNT5 > 0 THEN '02' -- 공동주택아니고 30임미만 1개이상시 불승인 WHEN MINWON_DOC_CD <> '6003' AND T_CNT6 > 0 THEN '02' -- 공동주택아니고 최저임금 1개이상시 불승인 WHEN MINWON_DOC_CD <> '6003' AND T_CNT1 > 0 AND T_CNT5 = 0 AND T_CNT6 = 0 THEN '01' -- 공동주택아니고 지원원별 승인 1개이상이고 최저임금, 30민미만이 없으면 승인(일부승인) WHEN MINWON_DOC_CD = '6003' AND T_CNT1 > 0 THEN '01' -- 공동주택이고 지원원별 승인 1개이상이면 승인(일부승인) ELSE '00' -- 해당하는 조건 없음 END AS RESULT FROM (SELECT COUNT(C.JEOPSU_NO) AS T_ALL -- 전체 , SUM(CASE WHEN A.SAEOPJANG_SIMSA_RESULT_CD IN ('01','04') THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS T_CNT1 -- 승인 , SUM(CASE WHEN A.SAEOPJANG_SIMSA_RESULT_CD IN ('02','05') THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS T_CNT2 -- 불승인 , SUM(CASE WHEN A.SAEOPJANG_SIMSA_RESULT_CD IN ('03','06') THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS T_CNT3 -- 보류 , SUM(CASE WHEN A.SAEOPJANG_SIMSA_RESULT_CD = '90' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS T_CNT4 -- 반려 , SUM(CASE WHEN A.MN30_MIMAN_FG IN ('02','05') THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS T_CNT5 -- 30인미만임금 불승인건 , SUM(CASE WHEN A.CHOEJEO_IMGEUM_FG IN ('02','05') THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS T_CNT6 -- 최저임금 불승인건 , MAX(B.MINWON_DOC_CD) AS MINWON_DOC_CD -- 민원서식 , MIN(A.SIMSA_JINHAENG_STATUS_CD) AS SIMSA_JINHAENG_STATUS_CD -- 심사진행상태 FROM US_IOWN.IJB050MT A JOIN US_IOWN.IAA100MT C ON C.ILJARI_NO = A.ILJARI_NO LEFT OUTER JOIN US_IOWN.IQA500MT B ON B.JEOPSU_NO = C.JEOPSU_NO WHERE A.DAEPYO_ILJARI_NO = :B1 -- 대표일자리번호 AND A.JIWON_YEAR = :B2 AND A.JEONGGI_CNT = :B3 AND A.SIMSA_CNT = (SELECT MAX(Z.SIMSA_CNT) FROM US_IOWN.IJB050MT Z WHERE Z.DAEPYO_ILJARI_NO = A.DAEPYO_ILJARI_NO AND Z.JIWON_YEAR = A.JIWON_YEAR AND Z.JEONGGI_CNT = A.JEONGGI_CNT ) )

SELECT /*+ PARALLEL(8) */ NVL(A1.SIDO , '기타지역') AS SIDO , NVL(A1.SIGUNGU_NM, '기타지역') AS SIGUNGU , MIN(A1.POST) AS POST , nvl(SUM(A1.SJ_CNT1), 0) + nvl(sum(A1.SJ_CNT2), 0) + nvl(sum(A1.SJ_CNT3), 0) + nvl(sum(A1.SJ_CNT4), 0) AS TOT_SINCHEONG_CNT , nvl(SUM(A1.SC_CNT1), 0) + nvl(sum(A1.SC_CNT2), 0) + nvl(sum(A1.SC_CNT3), 0) + nvl(sum(A1.SC_CNT4), 0) AS TOT_GEUNROJA_CNT , nvl(SUM(A1.SJ_CNT1), 0) AS SAEOPJANG_CNT1 , nvl(SUM(A1.SC_CNT1), 0) AS SINCHEONG_CNT1 , nvl(SUM(A1.SJ_CNT2), 0) AS SAEOPJANG_CNT2 , nvl(SUM(A1.SC_CNT2), 0) AS SINCHEONG_CNT2 , nvl(SUM(A1.SJ_CNT3), 0) AS SAEOPJANG_CNT3 , nvl(SUM(A1.SC_CNT3), 0) AS SINCHEONG_CNT3 , nvl(SUM(A1.SJ_CNT4), 0) AS SAEOPJANG_CNT4 , nvl(SUM(A1.SC_CNT4), 0) AS SINCHEONG_CNT4 FROM (SELECT /*+ FULL(Z) FULL(Z2) */ MIN(IZ.SIGUNGU_TITLE) AS SIGUNGU_NM , MIN(IZ.SIDO) AS SIDO , SUBSTR(IZ.SIGUNGU, 1, 2) AS POST , SAEOPJANG_GIJUN_NO , case when GYUMO_STR = '0004' then MAX(IV.COL1) end as SJ_CNT1 , case when GYUMO_STR = '0004' then SUM(IV.COL2) end as SC_CNT1 , case when GYUMO_STR = '0509' then MAX(IV.COL1) end as SJ_CNT2 , case when GYUMO_STR = '0509' then SUM(IV.COL2) end as SC_CNT2 , case when GYUMO_STR = '1030' then MAX(IV.COL1) end as SJ_CNT3 , case when GYUMO_STR = '1030' then SUM(IV.COL2) end as SC_CNT3 , case when GYUMO_STR = 'more' then MAX(IV.COL1) end as SJ_CNT4 , case when GYUMO_STR = 'more' then SUM(IV.COL2) end as SC_CNT4 FROM (SELECT /*+ FULL(A) FULL(B) FULL(D) FULL(G) FULL(E) */ NVL(NVL(B.ILJARI_NO, B.SAEOPJA_DRNO), G.P_MINWONIN_RGNO ) AS SAEOPJANG_GIJUN_NO , B.SAEOPJANG_POST , min( case when 1=1 then (select /*+ FULL(IJA113DT) */ case when count(distinct GEUNROJA_NO) < 5 then '0004' when count(distinct GEUNROJA_NO) < 10 then '0509' when count(distinct GEUNROJA_NO) < 30 then '1030' else 'more' end from IJA113DT where ILJARI_NO = B.ILJARI_NO and GY_STATUS_CD in ('0', '2')) end) as GYUMO_STR , MAX( CASE WHEN A.MINWON_DOC_CD IN ('6001', '6002', '6003') THEN 1 WHEN A.MINWON_DOC_CD = '6005' AND A.JEOPSU_FG = '3' THEN 1 WHEN A.MINWON_DOC_CD IN ('6004', '6005') AND A.JEOPSU_FG IN ('1', '4', '5', '6', 'D') THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) COL1 , SUM( CASE WHEN A.MINWON_DOC_CD IN ('6001', '6002', '6003') THEN (SELECT /*+ FULL(T1) */ COUNT(1) FROM TRADD891 T1 WHERE T1.PUBAP_ACPT_NO = E.PUBAP_ACPT_NO) + (SELECT /*+ FULL(T2) */ COUNT(1) FROM TRADD893 T2 WHERE T2.PUBAP_ACPT_NO = E.PUBAP_ACPT_NO) WHEN A.MINWON_DOC_CD IN ('6004', '6005') AND A.JEOPSU_FG IN ('4', '5') THEN NVL(TO_NUMBER(B.SAGEON_NO), 0) WHEN A.MINWON_DOC_CD = '6004' AND A.JEOPSU_FG IN ('1', '6', 'D') THEN (SELECT /*+ FULL(T1) */ COUNT(1) FROM IAA030MT T1 WHERE T1.JEOPSU_NO = A.JEOPSU_NO) + (SELECT /*+ FULL(T2) */ COUNT(1) FROM IAA040MT T2 WHERE T2.JEOPSU_NO = A.JEOPSU_NO) WHEN A.MINWON_DOC_CD = '6005' AND A.JEOPSU_FG IN ('1', '3', '6', 'D') THEN NVL(TO_NUMBER(B.SAGEON_NO), 0) ELSE 0 END) COL2 FROM IQA500MT A INNER JOIN IQA515DT B ON B.JEOPSU_NO = A.JEOPSU_NO INNER JOIN IQA501DT G ON G.JEOPSU_NO = A.JEOPSU_NO LEFT OUTER JOIN IQA525DT D ON D.JEOPSU_NO = A.JEOPSU_NO LEFT OUTER JOIN TRAAM800 E ON E.PUBAP_ACPT_NO = D.SIIS_YG_JEOPSU_NO LEFT OUTER JOIN TRADM890 F ON F.PUBAP_ACPT_NO = D.SIIS_YG_JEOPSU_NO AND F.ACPT_SEQ = 1 WHERE A.MINWON_DOC_CD IN ('6001', '6002', '6003', '6004', '6005') AND DECODE(A.MINWON_DOC_CD, '6004', '1', '6005', DECODE(A.JEOPSU_FG, '3', D.SIIS_YG_JEOPSU_NO, '1'), D.SIIS_YG_JEOPSU_NO) = DECODE(A.MINWON_DOC_CD, '6004', '1', '6005', DECODE(A.JEOPSU_FG, '3', E.PUBAP_ACPT_NO, '1'), E.PUBAP_ACPT_NO) AND A.JEOPSU_STATUS_CD NOT IN ('F', 'G') AND A.DELETE_YN = 'N' AND NOT EXISTS (SELECT /*+ UNNEST HASH_AJ FULL(B) */ 'X' FROM IQA500MT B WHERE A.JEOPSU_NO = B.JEOPSU_NO AND A.JEOPSU_STATUS_CD = '7' AND A.GYEOLJAE_STATUS_CD = '3') AND A.JEOPSU_DT BETWEEN '20171201' AND '20180524' AND A.GWANRI_JISA_CD <> '1000' GROUP BY NVL(NVL(B.ILJARI_NO, B.SAEOPJA_DRNO), G.P_MINWONIN_RGNO ), B.SAEOPJANG_POST ) IV LEFT OUTER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT Z.POST, Z.SIDO, Z2.SIGUNGU, Z2.SIGUNGU_TITLE FROM IQZ078CT Z LEFT OUTER JOIN IQZ079CT Z2 ON SUBSTR(Z.POST, 1, 3) = Z2.SIGUNGU AND Z2.SIGUNGU_FG = '4' ) IZ ON IZ.POST = IV.SAEOPJANG_POST GROUP BY IZ.SIGUNGU, SAEOPJANG_GIJUN_NO, GYUMO_STR ) A1 GROUP BY A1.SIDO, A1.SIGUNGU_NM ORDER BY 3, 1, 2

SELECT IV.GWANRI_JISA_CD , SF_ZA_GET_JISA_NM(IV.GWANRI_JISA_CD) AS GWANRI_JISA_NM , SUM(IV.COL1 + IV.COL2) AS TOT_ILJARI_SAEOPJANG_CNT , SUM(IV.COL3 + IV.COL4) AS TOT_ILJARI_SINCHEONG_CNT , SUM(IV.COL1) AS EDI_ILJARI_SAEOPJANG_CNT , SUM(IV.COL3) AS EDI_ILJARI_SINCHEONG_CNT , SUM(IV.COL2) AS GITA_ILJARI_SAEOPJANG_CNT , SUM(IV.COL4) AS GITA_ILJARI_SINCHEONG_CNT FROM ( SELECT NVL(NVL(B.SE_WONBU_NO, B.SAEOPJA_DRNO), G.P_MINWONIN_RGNO) AS SAEOPJANG_GIJUN_NO , A.GWANRI_JISA_CD , MAX(CASE WHEN A.MINWON_DOC_CD IN ('6001', '6002', '6003') AND E.PUBAP_ACPT_CD != 'NCP' THEN 1 WHEN A.MINWON_DOC_CD IN ('6005') AND A.JEOPSU_FG IN ('3') AND E.PUBAP_ACPT_CD != 'NCP' THEN 1 WHEN A.MINWON_DOC_CD IN ('6004', '6005') AND A.JEOPSU_FG IN ('4','5') THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) COL1 , MAX(CASE WHEN A.MINWON_DOC_CD IN ('6001', '6002', '6003') AND E.PUBAP_ACPT_CD = 'NCP' THEN 1 WHEN A.MINWON_DOC_CD IN ('6005') AND A.JEOPSU_FG IN ('3') AND E.PUBAP_ACPT_CD = 'NCP' THEN 1 WHEN A.MINWON_DOC_CD IN ('6004', '6005') AND A.JEOPSU_FG IN ('1','6','D') THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) COL2 , SUM(CASE WHEN A.MINWON_DOC_CD IN ('6001', '6002', '6003') AND E.PUBAP_ACPT_CD != 'NCP' THEN (SELECT COUNT(1) FROM TRADD891 T1 WHERE T1.PUBAP_ACPT_NO = E.PUBAP_ACPT_NO) + (SELECT COUNT(1) FROM TRADD893 T2 WHERE T2.PUBAP_ACPT_NO = E.PUBAP_ACPT_NO) WHEN A.MINWON_DOC_CD IN ('6004', '6005') AND A.JEOPSU_FG IN ('4','5') THEN NVL(TO_NUMBER(B.SAGEON_NO), 0) WHEN A.MINWON_DOC_CD IN ('6005') AND A.JEOPSU_FG IN ('3') AND E.PUBAP_ACPT_CD != 'NCP' THEN NVL(TO_NUMBER(B.SAGEON_NO), 0) ELSE 0 END) COL3 , SUM(CASE WHEN A.MINWON_DOC_CD IN ('6001', '6002', '6003') AND E.PUBAP_ACPT_CD = 'NCP' THEN (SELECT COUNT(1) FROM TRADD891 T1 WHERE T1.PUBAP_ACPT_NO = E.PUBAP_ACPT_NO) + (SELECT COUNT(1) FROM TRADD893 T2 WHERE T2.PUBAP_ACPT_NO = E.PUBAP_ACPT_NO) WHEN A.MINWON_DOC_CD = '6004' AND A.JEOPSU_FG IN ('1','6','D') THEN (SELECT COUNT(1) FROM IAA030MT T1 WHERE T1.JEOPSU_NO = A.JEOPSU_NO) + (SELECT COUNT(1) FROM IAA040MT T2 WHERE T2.JEOPSU_NO = A.JEOPSU_NO) WHEN A.MINWON_DOC_CD = '6005' AND A.JEOPSU_FG IN ('1','6','D') THEN NVL(TO_NUMBER(B.SAGEON_NO), 0) WHEN A.MINWON_DOC_CD = '6005' AND A.JEOPSU_FG IN ('3') AND E.PUBAP_ACPT_CD = 'NCP' THEN NVL(TO_NUMBER(B.SAGEON_NO), 0) ELSE 0 END) COL4 FROM IQA500MT A INNER JOIN IQA515DT B ON B.JEOPSU_NO = A.JEOPSU_NO INNER JOIN IQA501DT G ON G.JEOPSU_NO = A.JEOPSU_NO LEFT OUTER JOIN IQA525DT D ON D.JEOPSU_NO = A.JEOPSU_NO LEFT OUTER JOIN TRAAM800 E ON E.PUBAP_ACPT_NO = D.SIIS_YG_JEOPSU_NO LEFT OUTER JOIN TRADM890 F ON F.PUBAP_ACPT_NO = D.SIIS_YG_JEOPSU_NO AND F.ACPT_SEQ = 1 WHERE A.MINWON_DOC_CD IN ('6001', '6002', '6003', '6004', '6005') AND DECODE(A.MINWON_DOC_CD, '6004', '1', '6005', DECODE(A.JEOPSU_FG, '3', D.SIIS_YG_JEOPSU_NO, '1'), D.SIIS_YG_JEOPSU_NO) = DECODE(A.MINWON_DOC_CD, '6004', '1', '6005', DECODE(A.JEOPSU_FG, '3', E.PUBAP_ACPT_NO, '1'), E.PUBAP_ACPT_NO) AND A.JEOPSU_STATUS_CD NOT IN ('F','G') AND A.DELETE_YN = 'N' AND NOT EXISTS (SELECT 'X' FROM DUAL WHERE A.JEOPSU_STATUS_CD = '7' AND A.GYEOLJAE_STATUS_CD = '3') AND A.JEOPSU_DT BETWEEN '20180101' AND '20180524' AND A.GWANRI_JISA_CD <> '1000' GROUP BY NVL(NVL(B.SE_WONBU_NO, B.SAEOPJA_DRNO), G.P_MINWONIN_RGNO), A.GWANRI_JISA_CD ) IV GROUP BY IV.GWANRI_JISA_CD ORDER BY 1

INSERT INTO IKA050MT_IFS ( EAI_JEONSONG_SER , DAESANG_DATE , TOTAL_COUNT , DAY_COUNT , COUNT_RATE , INSERT_DATE , EAI_DML_YUHYEONG , EAI_SAENGSEONG_ILSI , EAI_JEONSONG_YN ) SELECT SQ_EIS_DAILY_JOB_SER.NEXTVAL AS EAI_JEONSONG_SER , TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE, 'YYYYMMDD'), 'YYYYMMDD') AS DAESANG_DATE , Y.NJ_CNT AS TOTAL_COUNT , Y.DI_CNT AS DAY_COUNT , DECODE(Y.BEF_CNT, 0, 0, NVL(ROUND(((Y.DI_CNT - Y.BEF_CNT)/Y.BEF_CNT)*100, 2), 0)) AS JG_CNT_PCT , SYSDATE AS INSERT_DATE , DECODE(NVL(Y.TODAY_YN, 'I'), 'Y', 'U', 'I') AS EAI_DML_YUHYEONG , SYSDATE AS EAI_SAENGSEONG_ILSI , 'N' AS EAI_JEONSONG_YN FROM (SELECT ZZ.DT , NVL(MAX(NJ_CNT),0) NJ_CNT , NVL(MAX(DI_CNT),0) DI_CNT , NVL(MAX(BEF_CNT),0) BEF_CNT , (SELECT 'Y' FROM IKA050MT_IFS C WHERE C.DAESANG_DATE = TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE, 'YYYYMMDD'), 'YYYYMMDD') AND ROWNUM = 1) AS TODAY_YN FROM ( SELECT '1' , TO_CHAR(SYSDATE,'YYYYMMDD') AS DT , COUNT(DISTINCT AA.ILJARI_NO ||AA.GEUNROJA_NO) AS NJ_CNT , 0 AS DI_CNT , 0 AS BEF_CNT FROM (SELECT D.ILJARI_NO, E.GEUNROJA_NO FROM (SELECT ILJARI_NO, JEOPSU_NO, SUM(JIGEUP_PRC) AS JIGEUP_PRC, MIN(FBS_JIGEUP_DT) AS FBS_JIGEUP_DT FROM IBC250MT WHERE FBS_JIGEUP_UIROE_FG = '2' AND FBS_JIGEUP_RESULT_CD = '0000' GROUP BY ILJARI_NO, JEOPSU_NO ) C , IBB010MT D , IBB020MT E WHERE D.JIGEUP_JEOPSU_NO = C.JEOPSU_NO AND E.JEOPSU_NO = D.JEOPSU_NO AND E.ILJARI_NO = D.ILJARI_NO AND E.JIWON_YEAR = D.JIWON_YEAR AND E.JIWON_MM = D.JIWON_MM AND E.JIWON_PRC_SANJENG_PRC > 0 AND C.FBS_JIGEUP_DT <= TO_CHAR(SYSDATE,'YYYYMMDD') UNION SELECT D.ILJARI_NO, SELECT NVL(A1.SIDO , '기타지역') AS SIDO , NVL(A1.SIGUNGU_NM, '기타지역') AS SIGUNGU , MIN(A1.POST) AS POST , SUM(A1.EDI_ILJARI_SAEOPJANG_CNT + A1.GITA_ILJARI_SAEOPJANG_CNT) AS TOT_ILJARI_SAEOPJANG_CNT , SUM(A1.EDI_ILJARI_SINCHEONG_CNT + A1.GITA_ILJARI_SINCHEONG_CNT) AS TOT_ILJARI_SINCHEONG_CNT , SUM(A1.EDI_ILJARI_SAEOPJANG_CNT) AS EDI_ILJARI_SAEOPJANG_CNT , SUM(A1.EDI_ILJARI_SINCHEONG_CNT) AS EDI_ILJARI_SINCHEONG_CNT , SUM(A1.GITA_ILJARI_SAEOPJANG_CNT) AS GITA_ILJARI_SAEOPJANG_CNT , SUM(A1.GITA_ILJARI_SINCHEONG_CNT) AS GITA_ILJARI_SINCHEONG_CNT FROM ( SELECT MIN(IZ.SIGUNGU_TITLE) AS SIGUNGU_NM , MIN(IZ.SIDO) AS SIDO , SUBSTR(IZ.SIGUNGU, 1,2) AS POST , SAEOPJANG_GIJUN_NO , MAX(IV.COL1) AS EDI_ILJARI_SAEOPJANG_CNT , SUM(IV.COL5 + IV.COL6 + IV.COL9) AS EDI_ILJARI_SINCHEONG_CNT , MAX(IV.COL3) AS GITA_ILJARI_SAEOPJANG_CNT , SUM(IV.COL7 + IV.COL8 + IV.COL10) AS GITA_ILJARI_SINCHEONG_CNT FROM ( SELECT NVL(NVL(B.SE_WONBU_NO, B.SAEOPJA_DRNO), G.P_MINWONIN_RGNO) AS SAEOPJANG_GIJUN_NO , B.SAEOPJANG_POST , MAX(CASE WHEN A.MINWON_DOC_CD IN ('6001', '6002', '6003') AND E.PUBAP_ACPT_CD != 'NCP' THEN 1 WHEN A.MINWON_DOC_CD IN ('6005') AND A.JEOPSU_FG IN ('3') AND E.PUBAP_ACPT_CD != 'NCP' THEN 1 WHEN A.MINWON_DOC_CD IN ('6004', '6005') AND A.JEOPSU_FG IN ('4','5') THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) COL1 , MAX(CASE WHEN A.MINWON_DOC_CD IN ('6001', '6002', '6003') AND E.PUBAP_ACPT_CD = 'NCP' THEN 1 WHEN A.MINWON_DOC_CD IN ('6005') AND A.JEOPSU_FG IN ('3') AND E.PUBAP_ACPT_CD = 'NCP' THEN 1 WHEN A.MINWON_DOC_CD IN ('6004', '6005') AND A.JEOPSU_FG IN ('1','6','D')
